2, 10).toUpperCase();\n        } else {\n          acctPwd = password; // 默认使用主密码\n        }\n        return {\n          post_id: post.id,\n          wechat_account_id: acct.account_id,\n          password: acctPwd\n        };\n      });\n      \n      await supabaseClient.from(\'daily_gallery_account_passwords\').upsert(accountPasswords);\n    }\n\n    // 触发自动补充待发布素材库（为下一轮发布做准备）\n    await supabaseClient.rpc(\'auto_refill_pending_daily_gallery_materials\');\n\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({\n        success: true,\n        message: \'发布成功\',\n        data: {\n          postId: post.id,\n          postDate: targetDate,\n          password: password,\n          imageCount: selectedImageIds.length,\n          expiresAt: passwordExpiresAt.toISOString()\n        }\n      }),\n      { headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' } }\n    );\n\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'[DailyGalleryPublish] Error:\', error);\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: error.message }),\n      { headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }, status: 500 }\n    );\n  }\n});\n'}]}

String(configValue.daily_random_keyword.keyword)) {\n      console.log(`[WechatLogic] Content matches today\'s random keyword: ${contentTrimmed}`);\n      return await handleDailyGalleryAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, platform, \'\');\n    }\n  }\n\n  // 1.5 处理硬编码的每日图集关键词 (迁移自 wechat-callback)\n  const passwordKeyword = configValue.password_keyword || \'今日图片\';\n  const serviceKeyword = configValue.service_auth_keyword || \'解锁\';\n  \n  const parseDate = (input: string): string | null => {\n    const year = today.split(\'-\')[0];\n    let match = input.match(/^(\\d{4})(\\d{2})(\\d{2})$/);\n    if (match) return `${match[1]}-${match[2]}-${match[3]}`;\n    match = input.match(/^(\\d{2})(\\d{2})$/);\n    if (match) return `${year}-${match[1]}-${match[2]}`;\n    match = input.match(/^(\\d{1,2})-(\\d{1,2})$/);\n    if (match) return `${year}-${match[1].padStart(2, \'0\')}-${match[2].padStart(2, \'0\')}`;\n    match = input.match(/^(\\d{1,2})月(\\d{1,2})日?$/);\n    if (match) return `${year}-${match[1].padStart(2, \'0\')}-${match[2].padStart(2, \'0\')}`;\n    return null;\n  };\n  const targetDate = parseDate(contentTrimmed);\n\n  if (contentTrimmed === passwordKeyword || contentTrimmed === serviceKeyword || contentTrimmed === \'今日\' || contentTrimmed === \'查询\' || contentTrimmed === \'帮助\' || contentTrimmed === \'签到\' || contentTrimmed === \'dl\' || contentTrimmed.includes(\'每日图片\') || contentTrimmed.includes(\'今日图片\') || targetDate) {\n    // 只有在以下情况下才拦截：\n    // 1. 开启了随机模式\n    // 2. 今天已有随机关键词\n    // 3. 用户发送的是固定关键词，或者是解析出的日期正是今天\n    const isTodayQuery = !targetDate || targetDate === today;\n    if (configValue.keyword_mode === \'random\' && configValue.daily_random_keyword?.date === today && isTodayQuery && (contentTrimmed === passwordKeyword || contentTrimmed === \'今日\')) {\n       console.log(`[WechatLogic] Blocking fixed gallery keyword "${contentTrimmed}" because today\'s random keyword is active.`);\n       return "💡 今日图集已开启【随机数字/关键词】模式，常规关键词（如\\"今日\\"）已暂时失效。\\n\\n请输入正确的随机数字获取今日内容。\\n\\n[提示] 往期内容不受影响，输入\\"月日\\"（如0504）或\\"年月日\\"（如20260504）即可查询今日之前的图集。";\n    }\n    \n    // 如果是"查询"或"帮助"，优先返回这些 action\n    if (contentTrimmed === \'查询\') return await handleAccountInfoAction(supabaseClient, openid);\n    if (contentTrimmed === \'帮助\') return `💡 常用指令指南：\\n\\n1️⃣ 发送"登录"：获取验证码登录账号。\\n2️⃣ 发送"今日图片"：查看今日推荐内容。\\n3️⃣ 发送"签到"：每日领取奖励。\\n4️⃣ 发送"查询"：查询您的积分和等级。`;\n    if (contentTrimmed === \'签到\') return await handleCheckInAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, \'\');\n    if (contentTrimmed === \'dl\') return await handleLoginAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, \'\');\n    \n    return await handleDailyGalleryAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, platform, \'\', targetDate);\n  }\n\n  let query = supabaseClient\n    .from(\'wechat_replies\')\n    .select(\'*\')\n    .eq(\'is_active\', true)\n    .eq(\'type\', \'keyword\')\n    .eq(\'platform\', platform);\n\n  if (configId) {\n    query = query.eq(\'config_id\', configId);\n  } else if (platform === \'miniprogram\') {\n    // 如果没有提供 configId 且是小程序，则尝试查找第一个有效的\n    const { data: mpConfig } = await supabaseClient\n      .from(\'miniprogram_configs\')\n      .select(\'id\')\n      .maybeSingle();\n    if (mpConfig) {\n      query = query.eq(\'config_id\', mpConfig.id);\n      configId = mpConfig.id; // 给后续 Action 使用\n    }\n  }\n\n  const { data: replies } = await query;\n\n  let matchedReply = null;\n  if (replies) {\n    // 先匹配全等\n    matchedReply = replies.find(r => r.match_type === \'exact\' && r.keyword?.toLowerCase() === contentLower);\n    // 再匹配模糊\n    if (!matchedReply) {\n      matchedReply = replies.find(r => r.match_type === \'fuzzy\' && contentLower.includes(r.keyword?.toLowerCase() || \'\'));\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (matchedReply) {\n    // 获取随机美图配置\n    const { data: beautyConfig } = await supabaseClient\n      .from(\'random_beauty_configs\')\n      .select(\'*\')\n      .maybeSingle();\n\n    let finalContent = matchedReply.reply_content;\n\n    // 随机美图变量替换\n    if (finalContent.includes(\'{{random.beauty_url}}\')) {\n      const { data: domainConfig } = await supabaseClient\n        .from(\'domain_configs\')\n        .select(\'domain_url\')\n        .eq(\'is_active\', true)\n        .limit(1)\n        .maybeSingle();\n      const baseUrl = (domainConfig?.domain_url || \'https://app-b5vwlh6eky69.appmiaoda.com\').replace(/\\/$/, \'\');\n      finalContent = finalContent.replace(/\\{\\{random\\.beauty_url\\}\\}/g, `${baseUrl}/refresh-image`);\n    }\n\n    if (finalContent.includes(\'{{openid}}\')) {\n      let opid = openid;\n      if (beautyConfig?.encrypt_openid !== false) {\n        opid = encodeOpenId(openid);\n      }\n      finalContent = finalContent.replace(/\\{\\{openid\\}\\}/g, opid);\n    }\n\n    if (finalContent.includes(\'{{random.beauty_count}}\') || finalContent.includes(\'{{random.beauty_limit}}\') || finalContent.includes(\'{{random.beauty_remaining}}\')) {\n      const today = new Date(new Date().getTime() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString().split(\'T\')[0];\n      const { data: usage } = await supabaseClient\n        .from(\'random_beauty_logs\')\n        .select(\'count\')\n        .eq(\'openid\', openid)\n        .eq(\'visit_date\', today)\n        .maybeSingle();\n      \n      const currentCount = usage?.count || 0;\n      \n      // 计算限额 (需要 profile)\n      const { data: profileForLimit } = await supabaseClient\n        .from(\'profiles\')\n        .select(\'role, group_id\')\n        .or(`mp_openid.eq.${openid},wechat_openid.eq.${openid}`)\n        .maybeSingle();\n      \n      let limit = beautyConfig?.default_limit ?? 8;\n      if (beautyConfig && beautyConfig.group_limits) {\n        const possibleKeys = [profileForLimit?.group_id, profileForLimit?.role, \'pt\'].filter(Boolean);\n        for (const key of possibleKeys) {\n          if (beautyConfig.group_limits[key as string] !== undefined) {\n            limit = beautyConfig.group_limits[key as string];\n            break;\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      finalContent = finalContent.replace(/\\{\\{random\\.beauty_count\\}\\}/g, currentCount.toString());\n      finalContent = finalContent.replace(/\\{\\{random\\.beauty_limit\\}\\}/g, limit.toString());\n      finalContent = finalContent.replace(/\\{\\{random\\.beauty_remaining\\}\\}/g, Math.max(0, limit - currentCount).toString());\n    }\n\n    // 通用变量替换\n    if (finalContent.includes(\'{{user.name}}\') || finalContent.includes(\'{user.name}\')) {\n      // 优先从 profiles 获取（支持自动创建的用户）\n      const { data: profile } = await supabaseClient\n        .from(\'profiles\')\n        .select(\'username\')\n        .or(`mp_openid.eq.${openid},wechat_openid.eq.${openid}`)\n        .maybeSingle();\n      \n      let nickname = profile?.username;\n      \n      // 兜底从 wechat_users 获取\n      if (!nickname) {\n        const { data: user } = await supabaseClient\n          .from(\'wechat_users\')\n          .select(\'nickname\')\n          .eq(\'openid\', openid)\n          .maybeSingle();\n        nickname = user?.nickname;\n      }\n      \n      finalContent = finalContent.replace(/\\{\\{user\\.name\\}\\}|\\{user\\.name\\}/g, nickname || \'亲爱的用户\');\n    }\n    \n    if (finalContent.includes(\'{{date.yyyy-mm-dd}}\') || finalContent.includes(\'{date.yyyy-mm-dd}\')) {\n      const today = new Date(new Date().getTime() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString().split(\'T\')[0];\n      finalContent = finalContent.replace(/\\{\\{date\\.yyyy-mm-dd\\}\\}|\\{date\\.yyyy-mm-dd\\}/g, today);\n    }\n\n    // 如果匹配到了关键词，且有分类 action，则执行对应逻辑\n    if (matchedReply.category && matchedReply.category !== \'none\') {\n      // 关键逻辑：如果开启了随机关键词模式，屏蔽常规"每日图集"动作的固定关键词\n      if (matchedReply.category === \'daily_gallery\' && configValue.keyword_mode === \'random\') {\n        console.log(`[WechatLogic] Blocking standard gallery keyword "${contentTrimmed}" because random mode is active.`);\n        return "💡 今日图集已开启【随机数字/关键词】模式，常规关键词（如\\"今日\\"）已暂时失效。\\n\\n请输入正确的随机数字获取内容。\\n[提示] 随机数字获取方式请见公众号最新推文或菜单。";\n      }\n      return await executeCategoryAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, matchedReply.category, platform, finalContent);\n    }\n    // 否则直接返回回复内容\n    return finalContent;\n  }\n\n  return null;\n}\n\nasync function executeCategoryAction(\n  supabaseClient: any,\n  configId: string,\n  openid: string,\n  category: string,\n  platform: string,\n  defaultReply: string\n) {\n  switch (category) {\n    case \'login\':\n    case \'binding\':\n      return await handleLoginAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, defaultReply);\n    case \'daily_gallery\':\n      return await handleDailyGalleryAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, platform, defaultReply);\n    case \'random_beauty\':\n      return await handleRandomBeautyAction(supabaseClient, openid, defaultReply);\n    case \'gallery_history\':\n      return await handleGalleryHistoryAction(supabaseClient, openid);\n    case \'account_info\':\n      return await handleAccountInfoAction(supabaseClient, openid);\n    case \'help\':\n      return defaultReply || `💡 常用指令指南：\\n\\n1️⃣ 发送"登录"：获取验证码登录账号。\\n2️⃣ 发送"每日图集"：查看今日推荐内容。\\n3️⃣ 发送"签到"：每日领取奖励。`;\n    case \'check_in\':\n      return await handleCheckInAction(supabaseClient, configId, openid, defaultReply);\n    default:\n      return defaultReply;\n  }\n}\n\nasync function handleLoginAction(supabaseClient: any, configId: string, openid: string, defaultReply: string) {\n  // 生成登录码逻辑 (复用原有逻辑)\n  const code = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000).toString();\n  const { data: domainConfig } = await supabaseClient\n    .from("domain_configs")\n    .select("domain_url, identifier")\n    .eq("is_active", true)\n    .limit(1)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  const siteUrl = domainConfig?.domain_url || "https://app-b5vwlh6eky69.appmiaoda.com";\n  const bindUrl = `${siteUrl}/login?bind_code=${code}&config_id=${configId}`;\n  \n  const { error } = await supabaseClient\n    .from("wechat_binding_requests")\n    .insert({\n      config_id: configId,\n      openid: openid,\n      code,\n      type: "wechat_to_user",\n      site_url: siteUrl,\n      domain_identifier: domainConfig?.identifier || "default",\n      expires_at: new Date(Date.now() + 10 * 60 * 1000).toISOString()\n    });\n\n  if (error) return "验证码生成失败，请稍后再试。";\n  \n  const baseReply = defaultReply || "您的登录验证码为：{code}\\n请在 10 分钟内完成登录。\\n\\n[方式1] 在 H5 的\\"登录/注册\\"中输入此验证码。\\n\\n[方式2] <a href=\\"{url}\\">点击此处直接登录</a>";\n\n  return baseReply.replace(\'{code}\', code).replace(\'{url}\', bindUrl);\n}\n\nasync function handleDailyGalleryAction(supabaseClient: any, configId: string, openid: string, platform: string, defaultReply: string, targetDate?: string | null) {\n  const beijingNow = new Date(new Date().getTime() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000);\n  const today = beijingNow.toISOString().split(\'T\')[0];\n  const queryDate = targetDate || today;\n  \n  // --- 关键优化：用户发送关键词时自动创建账户 ---\n  console.log(`[WechatLogic] Triggering auto-creation for ${openid} on keyword for date ${queryDate}, platform: ${platform}`);\n  const idField = platform === \'miniprogram\' ? \'mp_openid\' : \'wechat_openid\';\n  const createResult = await autoCreateUser(supabaseClient, openid, idField, \'daily_gallery_keyword\');\n  // --- 结束优化 ---\n\n  let nickname = \'亲爱的用户\';\n  if (createResult.is_new_user && createResult.user_info) {\n    nickname = createResult.user_info.username;\n  } else {\n    // 获取用户信息用于回复\n    const { data: profile } = await supabaseClient\n      .from(\'profiles\')\n      .select(\'username\')\n      .or(`mp_openid.eq.${openid},wechat_openid.eq.${openid}`)\n      .maybeSingle();\n    nickname = profile?.username || \'亲爱的用户\';\n  }\n\n  const { data: post } = await supabaseClient\n    .from(\'daily_gallery_posts\')\n    .select(\'id, password, is_published\')\n    .eq(\'post_date\', queryDate)\n    .eq(\'is_published\', true)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (!post) return `😔 抱歉，【${queryDate === today ? \'今日\' : queryDate}】图集内容尚未发布，请稍后再来。`;\n\n  // 获取访问链接基础 URL\n  const { data: galleryConfig } = await supabaseClient\n    .from(\'system_configs\')\n    .select(\'value\')\n    .eq(\'key\', \'daily_gallery_config\')\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  const configValue = galleryConfig?.value || {};\n  const redirectDomain = configValue.wechat_redirect_domain;\n  const includePasswordInReply = configValue.wechat_reply_include_password !== false;\n\n  let baseUrl = (redirectDomain || \'https://app-b5vwlh6eky69.appmiaoda.com/\').replace(/\\/$/, \'\');\n  \n  // 降级：如果没有配置自定义域名，尝试从 domain_configs 获取\n  if (!redirectDomain) {\n    const { data: domainConfig } = await supabaseClient\n      .from(\'domain_configs\')\n      .select(\'domain_url\')\n      .eq(\'is_active\', true)\n      .limit(1)\n      .maybeSingle();\n    if (domainConfig?.domain_url) {\n      baseUrl = domainConfig.domain_url.replace(/\\/$/, \'\');\n    }\n  }\n\n  // 获取/生成密码逻辑 (加入到随机密码库 daily_gallery_special_passwords)\n  const { data: userPwdRecord } = await supabaseClient\n    .from(\'daily_gallery_special_passwords\')\n    .select(\'*\')\n    .eq(\'creator_id\', openid)\n    .eq(\'target_date\', queryDate)\n    .eq(\'source\', \'wechat\')\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  let userPassword = userPwdRecord?.password;\n  let expiresAt = userPwdRecord?.expires_at;\n\n  if (!userPassword || new Date(expiresAt) < new Date()) {\n    userPassword = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000).toString();\n    \n    // 计算过期时间（明天晚上23:59:59）\n    const now = new Date();\n    const tomorrow = new Date(now);\n    tomorrow.setDate(tomorrow.getDate() + 1);\n    tomorrow.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);\n    expiresAt = tomorrow.toISOString();\n    \n    console.log(`[WechatLogic] Saving password for ${openid} on ${queryDate}: ${userPassword}`);\n    \n    // 同步到三个表\n    const results = await Promise.all([\n      supabaseClient\n        .from(\'daily_gallery_user_passwords\')\n        .upsert({\n          openid: openid,\n          post_date: queryDate,\n          password: userPassword,\n          expires_at: expiresAt,\n          locked_browser_id: null,\n          reset_count: 0\n        }, { onConflict: \'openid,post_date\' }),\n\n      supabaseClient\n        .from(\'daily_gallery_special_passwords\')\n        .upsert({\n          creator_id: openid,\n          target_date: queryDate,\n          password: userPassword,\n          expires_at: expiresAt,\n          source: \'wechat\',\n          password_type: \'periodic_single_user\',\n          is_one_time: false,\n          is_used: false,\n          max_usages: 999,\n          used_count: 0,\n          browser_id: null\n        }, { onConflict: \'creator_id,target_date,source\' }),\n\n      supabaseClient\n        .from(\'ad_unlock_logs\')\n        .insert({\n          item_id: queryDate,\n          unlock_type: \'daily_gallery\',\n          status: \'unlocked\',\n          openid: openid,\n          unlocked_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n          log_type: \'wechat_keyword_shared\',\n          success: true\n        })\n    ]);\n    \n    const syncError = results.find(r => r.error);\n    if (syncError) {\n      console.error("[WechatLogic] Failed to sync passwords:", syncError.error);\n    } else {\n      console.log("[WechatLogic] Successfully saved special password for user:", openid);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // 格式化有效期时间\n  const bj = new Date(new Date(expiresAt).getTime() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000);\n  const expiresTimeStr = `${bj.getUTCFullYear()}年${(bj.getUTCMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, \'0\')}月${bj.getUTCDate().toString().padStart(2, \'0\')}日 ${bj.getUTCHours().toString().padStart(2, \'0\')}:${bj.getUTCMinutes().toString().padStart(2, \'0\')}:${bj.getUTCSeconds().toString().padStart(2, \'0\')}`;\n\n  const encryptedOpenId = encodeOpenId(openid);\n  const accessUrl = `${baseUrl}/daily-gallery?date=${queryDate}&openid=${encryptedOpenId}&p=${userPassword}`;\n  \n  let baseReplyText = defaultReply;\n  if (!baseReplyText) {\n    baseReplyText = `📸 {nickname}，你好\\n【{date_text}】图集独立密码已发送\\n${includePasswordInReply ? \' 🔑 您的专属密码：{password}\\n\' : \'\'}⏰ 有效期至：{expire_time}\\n🔗 <a href="{url}">点击专属链接访问</a>\\n\\n💡 提示：此密码/链接仅供您在当前浏览器使用，转发无效。\\n\\n🔄 如果需要在其他浏览器查看请回复\\"重置看图密码\\"即可重置。`;\n  }\n  \n  return baseReplyText\n    .replace(\'{nickname}\', nickname)\n    .replace(\'{password}\', userPassword)\n    .replace(\'{date}\', queryDate)\n    .replace(\'{date_text}\', queryDate === today ? \'今日\' : queryDate)\n    .replace(\'{url}\', accessUrl)\n    .replace(\'{expire_time}\', expiresTimeStr);\n}\n\nasync function handleCheckInAction(supabaseClient: any, configId: string, openid: string, defaultReply: string) {\n  const beijingNow = new Date(new Date().getTime() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000);\n  const today = beijingNow.toISOString().split("T")[0];\n\n  // 1. 获取用户信息 (从 profiles)\n  const { data: profile } = await supabaseClient\n    .from("profiles")\n    .select("id, points, exp, custom_fields")\n    .or(`wechat_openid.eq."${openid}",mp_openid.eq."${openid}"`)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (!profile) return "⚠️ 请先在 H5 页面完成账号绑定后再进行签到。";\n\n  // 2. 检查今日是否已签到\n  const { data: existingCheckin } = await supabaseClient\n    .from("check_ins")\n    .select("id")\n    .eq("user_id", profile.id)\n    .eq("check_in_date", today)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (existingCheckin) {\n    return "🌟 您今天已经签到过了，明天再来吧！";\n  }\n\n  // 3. 执行签到 (获取连续签到天数，这里可以存放在 custom_fields 中)\n  const yesterdayStr = new Date(new Date(today).getTime() - 86400000).toISOString().split("T")[0];\n  const customFields = profile.custom_fields || {};\n  const lastCheckinStr = customFields.last_checkin_date || "";\n  \n  const newContinuous = (lastCheckinStr === yesterdayStr) ? (customFields.continuous_days || 0) + 1 : 1;\n  const earnedPoints = 10; // 默认奖励\n  const earnedExp = 5;\n\n  // 记录签到\n  await supabaseClient.from("check_ins").insert({\n    user_id: profile.id,\n    check_in_date: today\n  });\n\n  // 更新 profiles 用户数据\n  await supabaseClient.from("profiles").update({\n    points: (profile.points || 0) + earnedPoints,\n    exp: (profile.exp || 0) + earnedExp,\n    custom_fields: {\n      ...customFields,\n      last_checkin_date: today,\n      continuous_days: newContinuous\n    }\n  }).eq("id", profile.id);\n\n  const baseReply = defaultReply || "🌟 签到成功！您今日已完成签到。\\n\\n📅 连续签到：{days} 天\\n💰 获得奖励：{points} 积分\\n📈 当前成长：{exp} 点";\n\n  return baseReply\n    .replace(\'{days}\', newContinuous.toString())\n    .replace(\'{points}\', earnedPoints.toString())\n    .replace(\'{exp}\', earnedExp.toString());\n}\n\nasync function handleRandomBeautyAction(supabaseClient: any, openid: string, defaultReply: string) {\n  // 获取随机美图配置\n  const { data: config } = await supabaseClient\n    .from(\'random_beauty_configs\')\n    .select(\'*\')\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  // 获取用户信息以确定权限组\n  const { data: profile } = await supabaseClient\n    .from(\'profiles\')\n    .select(\'role, group_id\')\n    .or(`wechat_openid.eq.${openid},mp_openid.eq.${openid}`)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  // 获取域名配置\n  const { data: domainConfig } = await supabaseClient\n    .from("domain_configs")\n    .select("domain_url")\n    .eq("is_active", true)\n    .limit(1)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  const siteUrl = (domainConfig?.domain_url || "https://app-b5vwlh6eky69.appmiaoda.com").replace(/\\/$/, \'\');\n  \n  let opid = openid;\n  if (config?.encrypt_openid !== false) {\n    opid = encodeOpenId(openid);\n  }\n\n  const accessUrl = `${siteUrl}/refresh-image?openid=${opid}`;\n  \n  // 获取当前使用情况\n  const { data: usage } = await supabaseClient\n    .from(\'random_beauty_logs\')\n    .select(\'count\')\n    .eq(\'openid\', openid)\n sceneParts.join(\'&\').slice(0, 32);\n        page = config.login_page_path || "pages/user/wxlogin";\n      } else {\n        const shortItemId = (itemId || \'\').replace(/daily_gallery_/g, \'\').replace(/-/g, \'\').slice(0, 12);\n        // 生成确定性的校验码\n        const checkCode = await generateCheckCode(shortItemId);\n        // 生成唯一标识符以区分不同用户的扫码请求，解决并发扫码时的识别混乱问题\n        const uniqueToken = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6);\n        \n        let shortIdentifier = mpIdentifier;\n        // 激进缩写映射逻辑，以严格控制 scene 在 32 位限制内\n        if (shortIdentifier.includes(\'miaoda\') || shortIdentifier.startsWith(\'md-\')) shortIdentifier = \'md\';\n        else if (shortIdentifier.includes(\'supabase\') || shortIdentifier.startsWith(\'sp-\')) shortIdentifier = \'sp\';\n        else if (shortIdentifier.includes(\'wo58\') || shortIdentifier.startsWith(\'wo-\') || shortIdentifier.includes(\'dhso\')) shortIdentifier = \'wo\';\n        else if (shortIdentifier.includes(\'正式版\') || shortIdentifier === \'main\') shortIdentifier = \'ma\';\n        \n        const shortCheckCode = checkCode; // 已经在 generateCheckCode 中缩短了\n        const tinyToken = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 5); // 随机 token 缩短为 3 位\n        \n        if (shortIdentifier) {\n          // 场景格式: c=CHECK&d=ID&h=HOST&s=TOKEN\n          // 8 + 1 + 10 + 1 + 3 + 1 + 5 = 29 位 (c=123456&d=20260409&h=md&s=abc)\n          scene = `c=${shortCheckCode}&d=${shortItemId}&h=${shortIdentifier}&s=${tinyToken}`.slice(0, 32);\n        } else {\n          scene = `c=${shortCheckCode}&d=${shortItemId}&s=${tinyToken}`.slice(0, 32);\n        }\n        // 任务模式默认路径\n        page = config.task_page_path || "pages/user/task";\n      }\n      \n      console.log(`[WechatMP] Final scene: ${scene}, page: ${page}`);\n      \n      // 记录生成小程序码请求流水 (更新为 mp_qr_generation_logs)\n      await supabaseClient.from(\'mp_qr_generation_logs\').insert({\n    success: true,\n        ip_address: getClientIp(req),\n        openid: openid || body.openid || null, // 记录 openid\n        user_id: userId || body.userId || null, // 记录 user_id\n        details: {\n          action: \'generate_qr\',\n          type: type || (body.bindUserId ? \'bind\' : \'task\'),\n          itemId: itemId,\n          bindUserId: body.bindUserId,\n          browserId: body.browserId,\n          domain: domain,\n          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n        }\n      });\n      \n      const fetchQr = async (token: string, retry = true) => {\n        const qrUrl = `https://api.weixin.qq.com/wxa/getwxacodeunlimit?access_token=${token}`;\n        const qrBody = {\n          scene: scene,\n          page: page,\n          width: 430,\n          check_path: false,\n          env_version: "release"\n        };\n        \n        console.log("[WechatMP] Fetching QR from Wechat API...");\n        const qrRes = await fetch(qrUrl, {\n          method: "POST",\n          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n          body: JSON.stringify(qrBody)\n        });\n\n        const contentType = qrRes.headers.get("content-type");\n        if (contentType && contentType.includes("application/json")) {\n          const errorData = await qrRes.json();\n          console.error(`[WechatMP] Wechat API returned error JSON:`, errorData);\n          \n          // 如果 token 错误且允许重试，则强制刷新并重试一次\n          if (errorData.errcode === 40001 && retry) {\n            console.log("[WechatMP] Access token invalid (40001), retrying with forced refresh...");\n            const newToken = await getValidAccessToken(true);\n            return fetchQr(newToken, false);\n          }\n          \n          throw new Error(`Wechat API error (${errorData.errcode}): ${errorData.errmsg}`);\n        }\n\n        if (!qrRes.ok) {\n          const errorText = await qrRes.text();\n          console.error(`[WechatMP] QR Fetch failed with status      console.log("[WechatMP] QR fetched successfully. Converting to Base64...");\n      const qrBuffer = await qrRes.arrayBuffer();\n      const bytes = new Uint8Array(qrBuffer);\n      \n      // 使用更稳健的 Base64 转换方法，避免大数组解包导致的栈溢出\n      let binary = \'\';\n      for (let i = 0; i < bytes.byteLength; i += 1024) {\n        binary += String.fromCharCode(...bytes.slice(i, i + 1024));\n      }\n      const base64 = btoa(binary);\n      console.log(`[WechatMP] Base64 conversion complete. Length: ${base64.length}`);\n\n      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ \n        success: true, \n        qr_data: `data:image/png;base64,${base64}`,\n        scene: scene,\n        page: page\n      }), {\n        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n      });\n    }\n\n    // 获取小程序 OpenID (无感)\n    if (action === "get_openid" || action === "mp_login" || action === "mp_bind" || action === "get_login_token" || action === "mp_scan") {\n      let { code, bindUserId, ticket, scene, checkCode, hostIdentifier } = body;\n      \n      // 场景参数解析 (用于支持多端对接)\n      if (scene) {\n        console.log(`[WechatMP] Parsing scene: ${scene}`);\n        // 增加对 URL 编码的兼容处理\n        const decodedScene = scene.includes(\'%\') ? decodeURIComponent(scene) : scene;\n        decodedScene.split(\'&\').forEach((p: string) => {\n          const [k, v] = p.split(\'=\');\n          if (k === \'t\') ticket = v;\n          if (k === \'b\') bindUserId = v;\n          if (k === \'c\') checkCode = v;\n          if (k === \'h\') hostIdentifier = v;\n        });\n      }\n\n      if (action === "mp_scan") {\n        const finalTicket = ticket || body.ticket;\n        if finalTicket,\n            scene: scene || null,\n            ip_address: getClientIp(req),\n            log_type: \'mp_scan\',\n            success: true,\n            details: {\n              ua: req.headers.get("user-agent"),\n              timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            }\n          });\n          \n          console.log(`[WechatMP] Ticket ${finalTicket} marked as scanned`);\n        }\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true, version: "10.0.61" }), {\n          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n        });\n      }\n\n      console.log(`[WechatMP] Processed login params: ticket=${ticket}, bindUserId=${bindUserId}, host=${hostIdentifier}`);\n\n      if (!code && action !== "get_login_token") {\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Missing code" }), {\n          status: 400,\n          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n        });\n      }\n\n `https://api.weixin.qq.com/sns/jscode2session?appid=${config.app_id}&secret=${config.app_secret}&js_code=${code}&grant_type=authorization_code`;\n        const res = await fetch(url);\n        const req.headers.get("x-forwarded-for"),\n            details: {\n              errcode: data.errcode,\n              errmsg: data.errmsg,\n              timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            }\n          });\n          return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: data.errmsg }), {\n            status: 400,\n            headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n          });\n        }\n        mpOpenid = data.openid;\n      }\n\n      // 如果是登录行为 (小程序扫码登录授权)\n      if (action === "mp_login") {\n        if (!config.is_mp_login_enabled && !bindUserId) {\n          return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: "小程序登录功能未开启" }), {\n            headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n          });\n        }\n\n        // 核心安全验证: 验证校验码 (如果提供了 ticket/bindUserId 和 checkCode)\n        if ((ticket || bindUserId) && checkCode) {\n          // 统一处理逻辑：去除前缀、去除连字符、截取前12位，确保与生成逻辑一致\n          const rawId = (ticket || null,\n              scene: scene || null,\n              ip_address: req.headers.get("x-real-ip") || req.headers.get("x-forwarded-for"),\n              log_type: \'mp_login_check_error\',\n Date().toISOString()\n              }\n            });\n            \n            return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: "校验码验证失败" }), {\n              headers: {            .select(\'user_id\')\n            .ilike(\'ticket\', `${ticket.slice(0, 12)}%`)\n            .maybeSingle();\n          if (ticketRecord?.user_id) finalBindUserId = ticketRecord.user_id;\n        }\n\n        if (finalBindUserId) {\n           console.log(`[WechatMP] Auto binding openid ${mpOpenid} to user ${finalBindUserId}`);\n           const { error: bindError } = await console.error("[WechatMP] Auto bind error:", bindError.message);\n           } else {\n              // 绑定成功后，标记票据状态\n              if (ticket) {\n                 await supabaseClient.from(\'login_tickets\').update({\n                   status: \'fulfilled\',\n                   openid: mpOpenid,\n                   user_id: finalBindUserId,\n                   fulfilled_at: new Date().toISOString()\n                 }).ilike(\'ticket\', `${ticket.slice(0, 12)}%`);\n              }\n           }\n        }\n\n        // 先检查该 OpenID 是否已经绑定了系统账户 (用于前端辅助判断)\n   is_bound: !!user,\n          has_ticket: !!ticket,\n          has_bind: !!bindUserId,\n          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n          ua: req.headers.get("user-agent")\n        }\n query = query.eq(\'ticket\', ticket);\n          }\n          \n          const { error: fulfillError } = await query;\n          if (fulfillError) {\n             console.error("[WechatMP] Fulfill ticket error:", fulfillError.message);\n             // 如果绑定已经成功，这里就不强行报错了\n          }\n        }\n\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ \n          success: true, \n          message: bindUserId ?     });\n\n        if (linkError) {\n          console.error(`[WechatMP] GenerateLink error:`, linkError.message);\n          throw linkError;\n        }\n\n        console.log(`[WechatMP] Generated      // 某些版本的 Supabase 可能会将参数名设为 \'token\'\n        if (!token_hash) {\n          token_hash = url.searchParams.get(\'token\');\n        }\n\n        if (!token_hash) {\n          console.error(`[WechatMP] Could not find token_hash or token in generated link: ${linkData.properties.action_link}`);\n          // 记录获取令牌失败\n          await supabaseClient.from(\'mp_login_logs\').insert({\n            user_id: finalUserId,\n            log_type: \'h5_login_token_error\',\n            success: false,\n            ip_address:   await supabaseClient.from(\'mp_login_logs\').insert({\n          user_id: finalUserId,\n          log_type: \'h5_login_token_ready\',\n          success: true,\n          ip_address: req.headers.get("x-real-ip") || req.headers.get("x-forwarded-for"),\n          details: {\n            action: \'get_login_token\',\n            email: email,\n            timestamp: new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: "用户名或密码错误" }), {\n              headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n            });\n          }\n          bindId = (!currentBrowserId && scene) {\n        console.log(`[WechatMP] get_task_data: browserId missing, attempting to recover from scene: ${scene}`);\n        const decodedScene = scene.includes(\'%\') ? decodeURIComponent(scene) : scene;\n        const variants = [scene];\n        if (decodedScene !== scene) variants.push(decodedScene);\n\n        const { data: qrLog } = await supabaseClient\n          .from("mp_qr_generation_logs")\n          .select("details")\n          .in("scene", variants)\n          .order("created_at", { ascending: false })\n          .limit(1)\n          .maybeSingle();\n        \n        if (qrLog?.details?.browserId) {\n          currentBrowserId = qrLog.details.browserId;\n          console.log(`[WechatMP] get_task_data recovery success: browserId=${currentBrowserId}`);\n        } else {\n          // 兜底：尝试从旧的登录流水中查找 (兼容历史数据)\n          const { data: scanLog } = await supabaseClient\n            .from("mp_login_logs")\n            .select("details")\n            .eq("log_type", "scancode")\n            .eq("scene", scene)\n            .order("logged_at", { ascending: false })\n            .limit(1)\n            .maybeSingle();\n          \n          if (scanLog?.details?.browserId) {\n            currentBrowserId = scanLog.details.browserId;\n            console.log(`[WechatMP] get_task_data recovery from legacy log success: browserId=${currentBrowserId}`);\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (postError || !post) {\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: "发布记录不存在" }), {\n          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n        });\n      }\n\n      // 获取一张展示图片\n      if (post.image_ids && post.image_ids.length > 0) {\n        const { data: image } = await supabaseClient\n          .from("media_items")\n          .select("url, title, type, tags")\n          .eq("id", post.image_ids[0])\n          .single();\n        \n      if (image) {\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ \n          success: true, \n          data: { \n            image_url: image.url,\n            video_url: image.type === \'video\' ? image.url : null,\n            title: image.title || "今日赏析",\n            tags: image.tags || [],\n            itemId: postDate,\n            type: type || \'daily_gallery\'\n          } \n        }), {\n          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n        });\n      }\n      }\n\n      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: "无法获取预览图片" }), {\n        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n      });\n    }\n\n    if (action === "log_access") {\n      const { itemId, type, openid, userId, browserId } = body;\n      const identifier = (openid || userId || browserId);\n      \n      console.log(`[WechatMP] Logging access for itemId: ${itemId}, identifier: ${identifier}`);\n\n      // 统一标准化 itemId (日期格式)\n      const normalizedDate = normalizeDailyId(itemId);\n\n      const { error } = await supabaseClient\n        .from("daily_gallery_access_logs")\n        .insert({\n          publish_date: normalizedDate, // 统一使用 YYYY-MM-DD 格式\n          openid: identifier,\n          access_type: "view",\n          accessed_at: new Date().toISOString()\n        });\n\n      if (error) {\n        console.error("[WechatMP] Log access error:", error.message);\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: error.message }), {\n          status: 200,\n          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n        });\n      }\n\n      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true }), {\n        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n      });\n    }\n\n    if (action === "ad_callback") {\n      let { itemId, watch_status, checkCode, openid, userId, browserId, type, scene, hostIdentifier } = body;\n      \n      // 1. 优先从 scene 中解析 itemId（确保使用正确的日期）\n      if (scene) {\n        const decodedScene = scene.includes(\'%\') ? decodeURIComponent(scene) : scene;\n        const params = new URLSearchParams(decodedScene);\n        if (params.has(\'d\')) itemId = params.get(\'d\')!;\n        if (params.has(\'c\')) checkCode = params.get(\'c\')!;\n        if (params.has(\'h\')) hostIdentifier = params.get(\'h\')!;\n        console.log(`[WechatMP] Parsed scene: d=${itemId}, c=${checkCode}, h=${hostIdentifier}`);\n      }\n      \n      if (!itemId && !scene) throw new Error("Missing itemId and scene");\n\n      let currentBrowserId = browserId;\n      console.log(`[WechatMP] Ad callback: itemId=${itemId}, host=${hostIdentifier}, status=${watch_status}, browserId=${browserId}, scene=${scene}, checkCode=${checkCode}`);\n\n      // 2. 特殊处理：尝试通过 scene 或 itemId + checkCode 找回关联的 browserId\n      if (!currentBrowserId) {\n        console.log(`[WechatMP] browserId missing in body, attempting to recover from logs...`);\n        let recoveryToken = null;\n        if (scene) {\n          const decodedScene = scene.includes(\'%\') ? decodeURIComponent(scene) : scene;\n          const params = new URLSearchParams(decodedScene);\n          if (params.has(\'s\')) recoveryToken = params.get(\'s\')!;\n        }\n\n        // 尝试从生成码日志中恢复\n        let qrLogQuery = supabaseClient\n          .from("mp_qr_generation_logs")\n          .select("details, scene, created_at")\n          .order("created_at", { ascending: false });\n\n        if (recoveryToken) {\n           qrLogQuery = qrLogQuery.ilike("scene", `%s=${recoveryToken}%`).limit(1);\n        } else if (scene && scene.trim() !== "") {\n           const decodedScene = scene.includes(\'%\') ? decodeURIComponent(scene) : scene;\n           qrLogQuery = qrLogQuery.in("scene", [scene, decodedScene]).limit(1);\n        } else if (itemId && itemId.trim() !== "") {\n           const tenMinutesAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString();\n           qrLogQuery = qrLogQuery.gte("created_at", tenMinutesAgo).limit(100);\n        }\n\n        if (qrLogQuery) {\n          const { data: qrLogs } = await qrLogQuery;\n          if (qrLogs && qrLogs.length > 0) {\n             let matchedLog = null;\n             if (recoveryToken || (scene && scene.trim() !== "")) {\n                matchedLog = qrLogs[0];\n             } else if (itemId && itemId.trim() !== "") {\n                const shortItemId = itemId.replace(/daily_gallery_/g, \'\').replace(/-/g, \'\').slice(0, 12);\n                matchedLog = qrLogs.find(log => {\n                   const s = log.scene?.includes(\'%\') ? decodeURIComponent(log.scene) : log.scene;\n                   const matchId = s?.includes(`d=${shortItemId}`);\n                   const matchCode = checkCode ? s?.includes(`c=${checkCode}`) : true;\n                   return matchId && matchCode;\n                });\n             }\n             if (matchedLog?.details?.browserId) {\n                currentBrowserId = matchedLog.details.browserId;\n                console.log(`[WechatMP] RECOVERED browserId via log: ${currentBrowserId}`);\n             }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      const normalizedItemId = normalizeDailyId(itemId);\n      let currentUserId = userId;\n      let currentOpenid = openid;\n      const identifier = (openid || userId || currentBrowserId);\n\n      // 3. 数据对接增强\n      if (currentOpenid && !currentUserId) {\n        const { data: profile } = await supabaseClient.from("profiles").select("id").eq("mp_openid", currentOpenid).maybeSingle();\n        if (profile) currentUserId = profile.id;\n      }\n\n      // 4. 获取配置并处理解锁\n      const { data: configData } = await supabaseClient.from(\'system_configs\').select(\'value\').eq(\'key\', \'daily_gallery_config\').maybeSingle();\n      const dgConfig = configData?.value || {};\n      const adUnlockMode = dgConfig.ad_unlock_mode || \'direct\';\n      let generatedPassword = null;\n\n      const isCompleted = watch_status === \'completed\' || watch_status === \'completed_and_clicked\';\n      const logStatus = (isCompleted) ? "unlocked" : "watching";\n\n      // 无论哪种模式，只要看完广告，都生成一个 6 位数字密码作为备份/记录\n      if (isCompleted) {\n        generatedPassword = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000).toString();\n        \n        // 插入到特殊密码库（定期密码类型，2小时内可多次使用，但仅限第一个浏览器）\n        await supabaseClient\n          .from(\'daily_gallery_special_passwords\')\n          .insert({\n            password: generatedPassword,\n            target_date: normalizedItemId,\n            password_type: \'periodic_single_user\', // 定期密码\n            is_one_time: false, // 非一次性，2小时内可多次使用\n            max_usages: 999, // 不限次数\n            expires_at: new Date(Date.now() + 2 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString(), // 2小时内有效\n            source: \'miniprogram\',\n            creator_id: currentOpenid || \'unknown_mp_user\',\n            browser_id: currentBrowserId, // 绑定到第一个浏览器\n          });\n        \n        console.log(`[WechatMP] Generated periodic backup password ${generatedPassword} for date ${normalizedItemId}, browser: ${currentBrowserId}`);\n      }\n\n      const isActuallyUnlocked = isCompleted && adUnlockMode === \'direct\';\n      // 在密码模式下，看完广告也标记为 unlocked，表示该流程已完成且密码已生成\n      const finalLogStatus = (isActuallyUnlocked || (isCompleted && adUnlockMode === \'password\')) ? "unlocked" : "watching";\n\n      const insertData: any = {\n        item_id: normalizedItemId, // 使用修正后的 ID (YYYY-MM-DD)\n        unlock_type: type || "daily_gallery",\n        status: finalLogStatus,\n        watch_status: watch_status || "watching",\n        unlocked_at: isCompleted ? new Date().toISOString() : null,\n        created_at: new Date().toISOString(), // 强制更新创建时间\n        updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n        openid: currentOpenid,\n        user_id: currentUserId,\n        browser_id: currentBrowserId,\n        log_type: \'ad_callback\',\n        success: isCompleted,\n        details: {\n          body: body,\n          password: generatedPassword,\n          ad_unlock_mode: adUnlockMode,\n          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n          ip: getClientIp(req),\n          ua: req.headers.get("user-agent")\n        }\n      };\n\n      const { data: insertedData, error: logError } = await supabaseClient\n        .from("ad_unlock_logs")\n        .insert(insertData)\n        .select()\n        .single();\n\n      if (logError) {\n        console.error("[WechatMP] Ad callback log error:", logError.message);\n      }\n\n      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ \n        success: true, \n        data: insertedData || insertData,\n        password: generatedPassword, \n        message: generatedPassword ? `解锁码：${generatedPassword}` : \'解锁成功\'\n      }), {\n        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n      });\n    }\n\n    throw new Error(`Invalid action: ${action}`);\n\n  } catch (error: any) {\n    console.error("[WechatMP] Error:", error.message);\n    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: error.message }), {\n      status: 200, // 返回 200 以防前端因非 2xx 报错\n      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n    });\n  }\n});\n'}]}

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
import { createClient } from 'https://esm.sh/@supabase/supabase-js@2';

const corsHeaders = {
  'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type, x-api-key',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, DELETE, OPTIONS',
};

function createResponse(data, status = 200) {
  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {
    headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    status,
  });
}

function getSupabaseClient() {
  const url = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL') || '';
  const key = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') || '';
  return createClient(url, key);
}

async function validateRequest(supabase, url, req) {
  const apiKey = url.searchParams.get('apiKey') || req.headers.get('x-api-key') || '';
  const appId = url.searchParams.get('appId') || '';

  if (!apiKey || !appId) return { valid: false, message: 'Missing apiKey or appId' };

  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('app_api_keys')
    .select('id, permissions, expires_at')
    .eq('app_id', appId)
    .eq('api_key', apiKey)
    .eq('is_active', true)
    .maybeSingle();

  if (error || !data) return { valid: false, message: 'Invalid API Key' };
  return { valid: true, keyData: data };
}

Deno.serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });

  const url = new URL(req.url);
  const supabase = getSupabaseClient();
  const validation = await validateRequest(supabase, url, req);

  if (!validation.valid) {
    return createResponse({ success: false, message: validation.message }, 403);
  }

  const path = url.pathname;
  // 🔥 关键修复：兼容 action 参数
  const action = url.searchParams.get('action');

  try {
    // 🔥 修复：支持 ?action=list
    if (path.endsWith('/app-media') && action === 'list' || path.endsWith('/list')) {
      const page = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('page') || '0');
      const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '10');
      const type = url.searchParams.get('type') || 'all';
[The command completed with exit code 0.]

import React, { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface LazyImageProps extends React.ImgHTMLAttributes<HTMLImageElement> {
  src: string;
  thumbnailSrc?: string; // 缩略图URL（优先使用）
  lowQualitySrc?: string; // 低质量占位图（向后兼容）
  alt: string;
  className?: string;
  onLoad?: () => void;
  threshold?: number;
  rootMargin?: string;
  enableProgressiveLoad?: boolean; // 是否启用渐进式加载
}

/**
 * 懒加载图片组件
 * 支持：
 * 1. Intersection Observer API 实现视口外延迟加载
 * 2. 缩略图→原图渐进式加载
 * 3. WebP 格式优先
 * 4. 加载状态与错误处理
 */
export const LazyImage: React.FC<LazyImageProps> = ({
  src,
  thumbnailSrc,
  lowQualitySrc,
  alt,
  className = '',
  onLoad,
  threshold = 0.1,
  rootMargin = '50px',
  enableProgressiveLoad = true,
  ...props
}) => {
  // 优先使用缩略图，其次低质量图，最后为空
  const placeholderSrc = thumbnailSrc || lowQualitySrc || '';
  
  const [imageSrc, setImageSrc] = useState<string>(placeholderSrc);
  const [isLoaded, setIsLoaded] = useState(false);
  const [isThumbnailLoaded, setIsThumbnailLoaded] = useState(false);
  const [isFullImageLoaded, setIsFullImageLoaded] = useState(false);
  const [isInView, setIsInView] = useState(false);
  const [hasError, setHasError] = useState(false);
  const imgRef = useRef<HTMLImageElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!imgRef.current) return;

    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      (entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            setIsInView(true);
            observer.disconnect();
          }
        });
      },
      {
        threshold,
        rootMargin,
      }
    );

    observer.observe(imgRef.current);

    return () => {
      observer.disconnect();
    };
  }, [threshold, rootMargin]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isInView) return;

    // 如果有缩略图且启用渐进式加载
    if (enableProgressiveLoad && placeholderSrc && placeholderSrc !== src) {
      // 先加载缩略图
      if (!isThumbnailLoaded) {
        const thumbImg = new Image();
        thumbImg.src = placeholderSrc;
[The command completed with exit code 0.]

      setIsUploading(false);

  const handleVerify = useCallback(async (pwd?: string, cachedOpenid?: string | null) => {
    if (verifyingRef.current) return;
    
    // 防止过于频繁的并发请求
    if (Date.now() - lastVerifyTimeRef.current < 1500) {
      console.log('[DailyGallery] Verifying too frequent, ignoring...');
      return;
    }
    
    const passwordToVerify = pwd !== undefined ? pwd : password;
    
    console.log(`[DailyGallery] 开始验证密码... 日期: ${dateParam}, 密码: ${passwordToVerify ? '***' : '空'}, 是否微信: ${isWechat}`);
    
    if (!passwordToVerify.trim() && dgConfig.enable_password !== false) {
      toast.error((dgConfig.notification_messages?.empty_password) || '请输入访问密码');
      return;
    }

    // 优先使用 URL 中的 openid（用户从公众号或他人分享链接进入时携带）
    let effectiveOpenid = openidParam || cachedOpenid || null;
    
    // 其次尝试读取全局 openid 缓存（浏览器级持久化，不绑定日期）
    if (!effectiveOpenid) {
      try {
        const globalOpenid = localStorage.getItem('daily_gallery_openid');
        if (globalOpenid && globalOpenid !== 'unknown_user') {
          effectiveOpenid = globalOpenid;
          console.log('[DailyGallery] Using global cached openid from localStorage');
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[DailyGallery] Failed to read global openid:', e);
      }
    }
    
    // 最后尝试读取日期绑定的缓存 openid（兼容旧逻辑）
    if (!effectiveOpenid) {
      try {
        const cached = localStorage.getItem(`daily_gallery_${dateParam}`);
        if (cached) {
          const parsedCache = JSON.parse(cached);
          if (parsedCache.password === passwordToVerify && parsedCache.openid) {
            if (parsedCache.browserId && parsedCache.browserId !== browserId) {
              console.log('[DailyGallery] Cached browserId mismatch, clearing cache');
              localStorage.removeItem(`daily_gallery_${dateParam}`);
            } else {
              effectiveOpenid = parsedCache.openid;
              console.log('[DailyGallery] Using cached openid from localStorage for matching password');
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[DailyGallery] Failed to read cached openid:', e);
      }
    }

    // 如果 URL 中带有 openid，将其持久化到浏览器，便于下次自动使用
    if (openidParam) {
      try {
        localStorage.setItem('daily_gallery_openid', openidParam);
        console.log('[DailyGallery] Saved openid from URL to localStorage');
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[DailyGallery] Failed to save openid:', e);
      }
    }

    lastVerifyTimeRef.current = Date.now();
    setVerifying(true);
    try {
      const { data, error } = await api.supabase.functions.invoke('daily-gallery-verify', {
        body: {
          postDate: dateParam,
          password: passwordToVerify,
          openid: isWechat ? effectiveOpenid : effectiveOpenid,
          browserId: browserId,
          userId: user?.id
        }
      });

      const msgs = dgConfig.notification_messages || {};
      if (error) {
        let message = '网络或系统异常，请稍后重试';
        try {
          const errorText = typeof error?.context?.text === 'function' ? await error.context.text() : error?.message;
          // 处理 Lock broken 错误，将其转换为用户友好的提示
          if (errorText?.includes('Lock broken by another request')) {
             message = msgs.concurrent_request || '并发请求冲突，请 1 秒后重试';
             toast.error(message);
             return;
          }
          
          const errJson = JSON.parse(errorText || '{}');
          message = errJson.message || message;
          
          if (errJson.errorCode === 'BROWSER_LOCKED') {
            setShowResetOption(true);
            toast.error(msgs.browser_locked_title || '访问受限：浏览器已锁定', {
              description: errJson.message || (msgs.browser_locked_desc || '该密码已在其他浏览器中使用，专属密码仅支持首个打开的浏览器。'),
              duration: 5000
            });
            return;
          }

          if (errJson.errorCode === 'WECHAT_EXCLUSIVE_PASSWORD') {
            toast.error(msgs.wechat_exclusive_title || '访问受限：需专属链接', {
              description: errJson.message || (msgs.wechat_exclusive_desc || '该内容为专属访问，请通过公众号发送的专属链接打开。'),
              duration: 6000
            });
            return;
          }

          if (errJson.errorCode === 'DATE_MISMATCH') {
            toast.error(msgs.date_mismatch_title || '访问受限：日期不匹配', {
              description: errJson.message || (msgs.date_mismatch_desc || '该密码不适用于当前日期的图集，请获取今日正确密码。'),
              duration: 5000
            });
            return;
          }

          if (errJson.errorCode === 'PASSWORD_EXPIRED') {
            toast.error(msgs.password_expired_title || '访问受限：凭据已过期', {
              description: errJson.message || (msgs.password_expired_desc || '访问凭据已过期，请重新向公众号获取。'),
              duration: 5000
            });
            return;
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('Parse error text failed:', e);
          if (error.message?.includes('Lock broken')) {
            message = msgs.processing_request || '系统正在处理您的上一个请求，请稍后。';
          } else if (error.message?.includes('non-2xx')) {
            message = msgs.non_2xx_error || '密码验证失败，请确认密码是否正确';
          } else {
            message = error.message || message;
          }
        }
        
        toast.error(`${msgs.invalid_password_title || '验证失败'}: ${message}`);
        return;
      }

      const result = data;
      
      // 后端返回 ok 或 success 为 true 均视为成功
      if (result.status === 'ok' || result.success) {
        if (!isVerified) {
          const alreadyToast = sessionStorage.getItem(`daily_gallery_verified_${dateParam}`);
          if (!alreadyToast) {
            if (passwordToVerify === 'BYPASS_MP_UNLOCK') {
              toast.success(msgs.welcome_unlocked || '欢迎回来，今日内容已解锁', { duration: 2000 });
            } else {
              toast.success(msgs.welcome_verified || '验证成功！', { duration: 500 });
            }
          }
        }
        
        setIsVerified(true);
        const images = result.data?.images || [];
        setImages(images);
        console.log('[DailyGallery] 验证通过，已解锁图集内容', { imageCount: images.length });
        
        setPostInfo({
          postId: result.data?.postId,
          expiresAt: result.data?.expiresAt
        });

        localStorage.setItem(`daily_gallery_${dateParam}`, JSON.stringify({
          password: passwordToVerify,
          expiresAt: result.data?.expiresAt || new Date(Date.now() + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString(),
          openid: effectiveOpenid,
          timestamp: Date.now(),
          images
        }));

        // 将 openid 持久化到浏览器全局缓存，跨日期复用
        if (effectiveOpenid) {
          try {
            localStorage.setItem('daily_gallery_openid', effectiveOpenid);
          } catch (e) {
            console.error('[DailyGallery] Failed to save global openid:', e);
          }
        }
        
        sessionStorage.setItem(`daily_gallery_verified_${dateParam}`, 'true');

        await logAccess(result.data?.postId, passwordToVerify, result.data?.passwordType);
        
        /* 
        // 自动创建逻辑已取消
        if (result.is_new_user && result.user_info) {

          setNewPassword('');
          setConfirmPassword('');

        }
        */
        
        // 验证成功后，刷新已读记录
        if (typeof fetchReadHistory === 'function') fetchReadHistory();
        if (typeof fetchSeenMediaIds === 'function') fetchSeenMediaIds();
        return;
      }
      
      if (!result.success) {
        console.warn('[DailyGallery] 验证未通过:', result.message, { errorCode: result.errorCode });
        // 记录失败的密码和时间，避免频繁自动重试导致 UI 震荡

        lastFailedTimeRef.current = Date.now();

          console.log('[DailyGallery] Silent MP unlock check returned success:false');

        thumbImg.src = placeholderSrc;
        thumbImg.onload = () => {
          setImageSrc(placeholderSrc);
          setIsThumbnailLoaded(true);
        };
        thumbImg.onerror = () => {
          console.error(`Failed to load thumbnail: ${placeholderSrc}`);
          // 缩略图加载失败，直接加载原图

  const loadFullImage = () => {
    const img = new Image();
    img.src = src;
    img.onload = () => {
      setImageSrc(src);
      setIsFullImageLoaded(true);
      setIsLoaded(true);
      onLoad?.();
    };
    img.onerror = () => {
      console.error(`Failed to load image: ${src}`);
      setHasError(true);
      setIsLoaded(true);
    };
  };

  return (
    <div className={cn('relative overflow-hidden bg-muted', className)}>
      {/* 占位符 */}
      {!isLoaded && !hasError && (
        <div className="absolute inset-0 animate-pulse bg-muted" />
      )}

      {/* 图片 */}
      <img
        ref={imgRef}
        src={imageSrc}
        alt={alt}
        className={cn(
          'w-full h-full object-contain transition-opacity duration-500',
          isLoaded ? 'opacity-100' : 'opacity-50',
          className
        )}
        loading="lazy"
        {...props}
      />

      {/* 错误状态 */}
      {hasError && (
        <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-muted text-muted-foreground">
          <span className="text-sm">加载失败</span>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

import React, { forwardRef, useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { Loader2, AlertCircle, Camera, RefreshCw, ShieldCheck, ImageOff, Image as ImageIcon } from 'lucide-react';
import { getProtectedUrl, getImageUrl, getZoneramaProxyUrl, optimizeXiaohongshuUrl, getOptimizedImageUrl, applyImageProcessing } from '@/lib/media';
import { useConfig } from '@/contexts/ConfigContext';

import { debugLogEmitter } from './DebugLogOverlay';


const SlicedImage = ({ 
  urls, 
  alt, 
  className, 
  mode,
  onLoad, 
  onError 
}: { 
  urls: string[], 
  alt?: string, 
  className?: string, 
  mode: 'blob_slice' | 'canvas_slice' | 'canvas',
  onLoad?: (dimensions?: { width: number, height: number }) => void, 
  onError?: () => void 
}) => {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement | null>(null);
  
  // 提取外部传入的 object-fit 类名
  const objectFitClass = className?.includes('object-cover') ? 'object-cover' : 'object-contain';
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (urls.length === 0) return;
    let active = true;
    if (urls.length === 1) {
      const img = new Image();
      img.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
      img.referrerPolicy = 'no-referrer';
      img.onload = () => {
        if (!active) return;
        const canvas = canvasRef.current;
        if (!canvas) return;
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        if (!ctx) return;

        const w = img.naturalWidth;
        const h = img.naturalHeight;
        canvas.width = w;
        canvas.height = h;

        if (mode === 'canvas') {
          // 完整绘制
          ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h);
        } else {
          // 在单个 Canvas 内部进行分片绘制，消除 DOM 间隙
          const leftWidth = Math.floor(w / 2);
          const rightWidth = w - leftWidth;
          const topHeight = Math.floor(h / 2);
          const bottomHeight = h - topHeight;

          // 绘制左上
          ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, leftWidth, topHeight, 0, 0, leftWidth, topHeight);
          // 绘制右上
          ctx.drawImage(img, leftWidth, 0, rightWidth, topHeight, leftWidth, 0, rightWidth, topHeight);
          // 绘制左下
          ctx.drawImage(img, 0, topHeight, leftWidth, bottomHeight, 0, topHeight, leftWidth, bottomHeight);
          // 绘制右下
          ctx.drawImage(img, leftWidth, topHeight, rightWidth, bottomHeight, leftWidth, topHeight, rightWidth, bottomHeight);
        }
        onLoad?.();
      };
      img.onerror = () => { if (active) onError?.(); };
      img.src = urls[0];
      return () => { active = false; };
    }
    return () => { active = false; };
  }, [urls, mode, onLoad, onError]);

  return (
    <div 
      ref={containerRef}
      className={cn(className, "relative overflow-hidden select-none flex items-center justify-center")}
      onContextMenu={(e) => e.preventDefault()}
    >
      <canvas 
        ref={canvasRef}
        aria-label={alt}
        role="img"
        className={cn("w-full h-full pointer-events-none", objectFitClass)}
        style={{ display: 'block' }}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';

// 全局静态缓存，用于追踪本会话已成功加载的资源
const globalLoadedSrcs = new Set<string>();

export const isMediaCached = (src: string | null | undefined) => {
  if (!src) return false;
  return globalLoadedSrcs.has(src);
};

    // 全局 Zonerama 代理处理
    const zoneramaAuth = authToken || (config as any)?.zonerama_auth; // 优先使用属性传入的 auth，其次全局
    const thumbOptions = isThumbnail ? { 
      width: config?.thumbnail_width || 400, 
      quality: config?.thumbnail_quality || 60 
    } : {};
    
    const finalSrcRaw = getZoneramaProxyUrl(normalizedSrc, zoneramaAuth, albumId, thumbOptions);

    if ((config?.enable_progressive_loading !== false) && !isThumbnail) {
      // 1. 优先生成过渡图（超低分辨率，几乎瞬间加载）
      const tUrl = applyImageProcessing(normalizedSrc, config || null, '过渡');
      setTransitionUrl(tUrl);

      // 2. 处理缩略图
      if (thumbnailSrc) {
        // 如果指定了 thumbnailRuleKey（如 '首瀑'），则生成与瀑布流完全一致的 URL，命中浏览器缓存
        const finalThumbSrc = thumbnailRuleKey 
          ? applyImageProcessing(thumbnailSrc, config || null, thumbnailRuleKey)
          : thumbnailSrc;
        
        setProtectedThumbnailUrl(finalThumbSrc); 
        // 异步尝试转为加密链接，提升安全性
        getProtectedUrl(finalThumbSrc, finalUseWebp, { quality: 30 }).then(url => { if (active) setProtectedThumbnailUrl(url); });
      }
    }
    if (!configLoading) {
      const loadMainContent = () => {
        if (!active) return;
        const optParams: any = { 
          enableBlob: config?.enable_blob !== false, 
          enableCache: config?.enable_image_cache === true, 
          version, 
          priority,
          config: config || null
        };
        if (isThumbnail) {
          optParams.width = config?.thumbnail_width || 300;
          optParams.quality = config?.thumbnail_quality ?? 40;
        }
        const mode = forceMode || securityConfig?.mode || (config?.enable_blob !== false ? 'blob' : 'original');
        // HLS 视频（m3u8）无法通过 Blob 加载，必须使用 original 模式
        const isHLS = src.toLowerCase().includes('.m3u8');
        const effectiveMode = isHLS ? 'original' : mode;
        setCurrentMode(effectiveMode);
        
        if ((effectiveMode === 'blob_slice' || effectiveMode === 'canvas_slice') && type === 'image') {
          const finalSrc = getImageUrl(finalSrcRaw, isThumbnail, config, albumId, ruleKey);
          detectFeatures(finalSrc);
          if (effectiveMode === 'blob_slice') {
            getProtectedUrl(finalSrc, finalUseWebp, optParams).then((url) => { 
              if (active) { 
                setSliceUrls([url]); 
                setProtectedUrl(url); 
              } 
            }).catch(() => { if (active) setProtectedUrl(finalSrcRaw || null); });
          } else {
            setSliceUrls([finalSrc]); 
            setProtectedUrl(finalSrc); 
          }
        } else if (effectiveMode === 'canvas' && type === 'image') {
          const finalSrc = getImageUrl(finalSrcRaw, isThumbnail, config, albumId, ruleKey);
          detectFeatures(finalSrc);
          setSliceUrls([finalSrc]); 
          setProtectedUrl(finalSrc);
        } else if (effectiveMode === 'original') {
          const finalSrc = getImageUrl(finalSrcRaw, isThumbnail, config, albumId, ruleKey);
          detectFeatures(finalSrc);
          setProtectedUrl(finalSrc); 
          setSliceUrls([]);
        } else {
          // blob 模式
          const finalSrc = getImageUrl(finalSrcRaw, isThumbnail, config, albumId, ruleKey);
          detectFeatures(finalSrc);
          setSliceUrls([]);
          getProtectedUrl(finalSrc, finalUseWebp, optParams).then((url) => { if (active) setProtectedUrl(url); }).catch(() => { if (active) setProtectedUrl(finalSrc || null); });
        }
      };

      if (priority || isThumbnail) {
        loadMainContent();
      } else {
        // 非优先级且非缩略图的资源（即大图/详情图），延迟加载以确保首屏/可视区域资源优先
        const delay = (window as any)._is_initial_load !== false ? 800 : 300;
        const timer = setTimeout(loadMainContent, delay);
        (window as any)._is_initial_load = false;
        return () => clearTimeout(timer);
      }
